POLICY</span></strong></p> <p class="c14 c28"> </p><h4 id="h.tto7xqrbqfk4" class="c10 c31"><span class="c5">INTRODUCTION</span></h4> <p class="c17"> </p><p class="c10"><span class="c1">This privacy policy (</span><span class="c6">Privacy Policy</span><span class="c1">) specifies how Viewport Pty Ltd (ACN 608 647 418) (</span><span class="c6">Viewport</span><span class="c1">, </span><span class="c6">us</span><span class="c1">, </span><span class="c6">we</span><span class="c1"> or </span><span class="c6">our</span><span class="c1">) collects, stores, uses and discloses your personal information. By using any of our websites, applications (IOS and Android) or our other products (together referred to as </span><span class="c6">the Platforms</span><span class="c0">), making use of our services or applying for a job with us you accept this Privacy Policy. </span></p> <p class="c2"> </p><p class="c10"><span class="c0">We may amend this Privacy Policy from time to time as our business requires or the law changes. If we do, the new Privacy Policy will be posted on, or notified via, the Platforms. Your continued use of any Platform and / or our services will constitute your acceptance of any changes. If you object to any changes to the Privacy Policy, you must stop using the Platforms and our services. </span></p> <p id="h.30j0zll" class="c2"> </p><p class="c10 nitro-offscreen"><span class="c1">Dated 2/12/2020</span><span class="c1">. </span></p> <p class="c17"> </p><ol class="c4 lst-kix_list_39-0 start nitro-offscreen" start="1"> <li class="c8"> <h4 id="h.1fob9te" style="display:inline;"><span class="c5">PERSONAL INFORMATION</span></h4> </li> </ol> <p class="c10 c15 nitro-offscreen"><span class="c1">When used in this Privacy Policy, the term </span><span class="c6">personal information</span><span class="c1"> has the meaning given to it in the </span><span class="c1 c12">Privacy Act 1988</span><span class="c1">&nbsp;(Cth) (</span><span class="c6">Privacy Act</span><span class="c0">). In general terms, it is any information that can be used to personally identify you.</span></p> <p class="c2"> </p><ol class="c4 lst-kix_list_39-0 nitro-offscreen" start="2"> <li class="c8"> <h4 id="h.3znysh7" style="display:inline;"><span class="c5">PERSONAL INFORMATION WE COLLECT </span></h4> </li> </ol> <p class="c10 c15 nitro-offscreen"><span class="c6 c12">Information you give us</span></p> <ol class="c4 lst-kix_list_39-1 start nitro-offscreen" start="1"> <li class="c3"><span class="c0">The types of personal information that we collect about you will depend on our relationship with you, the circumstances of collection and / or the type of products and services you request from us. The personal information may include (but is not limited to):</span></li> </ol> <ol class="c4 lst-kix_list_5-0 start nitro-offscreen" start="1"> <li class="c7"><span class="c0">your name, gender and date of birth; </span></li> <li class="c7"><span class="c0">your contact details including your email address, postal / delivery address and telephone / mobile number; </span></li> <li class="c7"><span class="c0">billing information and credit card information; </span></li> <li class="c7"><span class="c0">photographs and videos;</span></li> <li class="c7"><span class="c0">details of the products and services you have purchased from us or which you have enquired about, together with any additional information necessary to deliver those products and services and to respond to your enquiries;</span></li> <li class="c7"><span class="c0">information you provide to us through our service centre, customer surveys or discussions with our representatives from time to time; and / or </span></li> <li class="c7"><span class="c0">additional information relating to you that you provide to us directly or indirectly through our Platforms or otherwise.</span></li> </ol> <ol class="c4 lst-kix_list_39-1 start nitro-offscreen" start="1"> <li class="c3"><span class="c0">If you apply for a job with us, we may collect the following personal information, in addition to the information referred to in paragraph 2.1:</span></li> </ol> <ol class="c4 lst-kix_list_41-0 start nitro-offscreen" start="1"> <li class="c10 c24"><span class="c0">citizenship status; </span></li> <li class="c7"><span class="c0">curriculum vitae or resume;</span></li> <li class="c7"><span class="c0">employment history;</span></li> <li class="c7"><span class="c0">academic records and qualifications; and</span></li> <li class="c7"><span class="c0">referee details and comments made by referees about you.</span></li> </ol> <p class="c10 c15 nitro-offscreen"><span class="c6 c12 c20">Information you disclose using Interactive Services</span></p> <ol class="c4 lst-kix_list_39-1 nitro-offscreen" start="2"> <li class="c3"><span class="c0">The Platforms include user-generated profiles, interactive messaging services and webcam services (</span><span class="c5">Interactive Services</span><span class="c0">). These are designed to enable you to communicate with other users of the Platforms (</span><span class="c5">Other Users</span><span class="c0">). </span></li> <li class="c3"><span class="c0">Information that is disclosed by you during your use of the Interactive Services may be seen, copied and used by us and Other Users. There is no expectation of privacy when using the Interactive Services and we have no control over how Other Users may use the information you disclose. You should exercise caution and discretion before deciding to disclose that information.</span></li> </ol> <p class="c2 c19"> </p><p class="c2 c19"> </p><p class="c10 c19 nitro-offscreen"><span class="c6 c20 c12">Information given to us by third-parties</span></p> <ol class="c4 lst-kix_list_39-1 nitro-offscreen" start="4"> <li class="c3"><span class="c0">We may collect information about you which we have received from third-parties. For example, if you access a Platform through a third-party connection or log-in, such as Facebook Connect, that third-party may pass some information about your use of its services to us. This information may include (but is not limited to):</span></li> </ol> <ol class="c4 lst-kix_list_15-0 start nitro-offscreen" start="1"> <li class="c7"><span class="c1">an ID associated with your third-party account;</span></li> <li class="c7"><span class="c0">any information you have permitted the third-party to share with us; and/or</span></li> <li class="c7"><span class="c1">any information you have made public in connection with the third-party provider.</span></li> </ol> <p class="c10 c19 nitro-offscreen"><span class="c6 c20 c12">Location information</span></p> <ol class="c4 lst-kix_list_39-1 nitro-offscreen" start="5"> <li class="c3"><span class="c0">We may collect additional information from you. For example, we may collect your devices operating system, the name of your mobile carrier and network, details of your location, and with your permission your GPS/geo-location. </span></li> <li class="c3"><span class="c0">The degree to which your location can be identified depends on the device you are using (e.g. smart phone, tablet, laptop or desktop). We collect this information in order to provide you with the best level of service. If you enable location services, we may collect location data periodically as you use or leave open your access to a Platform. We may also use this data internally or in conjunction with our third-party service providers to customise your experience and provide offers that may be relevant to you. Depending on the service you use (e.g. Apple OSX iOS, Windows, Android etc) to access a Platform you may be able to control, from within your devices settings, whether you wish to share your location data with us.</span></li> </ol> <p class="c2"> </p><ol class="c4 lst-kix_list_39-0 nitro-offscreen" start="3"> <li class="c8"> <h4 id="h.2et92p0" style="display:inline;"><span class="c6 c26">HOW WE COLLECT PERSONAL INFORMATION</span></h4> </li> </ol> <ol class="c4 lst-kix_list_39-1 start nitro-offscreen" start="1"> <li class="c3"><span class="c0">We may collect personal information about you:</span></li> </ol> <ol class="c4 lst-kix_list_28-0 start nitro-offscreen" start="1"> <li class="c7"><span class="c1">if you register an account (</span><span class="c6">Account</span><span class="c0">), including by creating a username and password, on a Platform;</span></li> <li class="c7"><span class="c0">through your access and use of the Platforms and our services;</span></li> <li class="c7"><span class="c0">if you send us an email / message or otherwise interact with us including during conversations between you and our representatives; and/or</span></li> <li class="c7"><span class="c0">third-party companies, like Facebook, who share your information with us in order to make your online experience more seamless.</span></li> </ol> <ol class="c4 lst-kix_list_39-1 start nitro-offscreen" start="1"> <li class="c3"><span class="c0">We use a range of social media channels (</span><span class="c5">Social Media</span><span class="c0">) to distribute news, announcements, promotions and to address community enquiries. If you submit or post comments, images, tweets, recordings or other personal content for public display on Social Media, that information may be available for anyone in the world to read, view or comment on. We are not responsible to you for the information handling practices of Social Media.</span></li> <li class="c3"><span class="c0">If you provide information to us about a third party (including a friend, family member, colleague and / or associate), you must ensure that you are entitled to disclose that information to us and that, without the need to take further steps pursuant to privacy laws, we may collect, use and disclose such information for the purposes set out in this Privacy Policy. The party concerned should be aware of this Privacy Policy and consent to how we will use the information relating to them as set out in this policy. &nbsp;</span></li> </ol> <p class="c2 c22"> </p><p class="nitro-offscreen">&nbsp;</p> <ol class="c4 lst-kix_list_39-0 nitro-offscreen" start="4"> <li class="c8"> <h4 id="h.1t3h5sf" style="display:inline;"><span class="c5">HOW WE USE YOUR PERSONAL </span></li> <li class="c3"><span class="c0">for the purposes of a confidential alternative dispute resolution; and/or</span></li> <li class="c3"><span class="c0">as otherwise required or permitted by any law (including the Privacy Act).</span></li> </ol> <p class="c2 c22"> </p><ol class="c4 lst-kix_list_39-0 nitro-offscreen" start="6"> <li class="c8"> <h4 id="h.2s8eyo1" style="display:inline;"><span class="c6 c26">WHAT IF WE CANT COLLECT YOUR PERSONAL INFORMATION </span></h4> </li> </ol> <p class="c10 c15 nitro-offscreen"><span class="c0">If you do not provide us with the information described in this Privacy Policy, some or all of the following may happen:</span></p> <ol class="c4 lst-kix_list_39-1 nitro-offscreen" start="9"> <li class="c3"><span class="c0">We may not be able to provide you with the products or services you requested, either to the same standard, or at all;</span></li> <li class="c3"><span class="c0">We may not be able to provide you with information about products and services that you may want, including information about discounts sales or special promotions; and/or</span></li> <li class="c3"><span class="c0">We may be unable to tailor the content of our Platforms and your preferences and your experience of our websites and applications may not be as enjoyable or useful.</span></li> </ol> <p class="c2 c22"> </p><p class="nitro-offscreen">&nbsp;</p> <ol class="c4 lst-kix_list_39-0 nitro-offscreen" start="7"> <li class="c8"> <h4 id="h.3rdcrjn" style="display:inline;"><span class="c5">ACCESSING AND CORRECTING YOUR PERSONAL INFORMATION </span></h4> </li> </ol> <ol class="c4 lst-kix_list_39-1 start nitro-offscreen" start="1"> <li id="h.26in1rg" class="c3"><span class="c0">You may request access to any personal information we hold about you at any time by contacting us (details at section 9 below). Where we hold information that you are entitled to access, we will try to provide you with suitable means of accessing it (for example, by mailing or emailing it to you). We will not charge for simply making a request and will not charge for making any corrections to your personal information. If you make an access request, we will ask you to verify your identity. There may be instances where we cannot grant you access to the personal information we hold. For example, we may need to refuse access if granting access would interfere with the privacy of others, or if it would result in a breach of confidentiality. If that happens, we will give you reasons for any refusal.</span></li> <li class="c3"><span class="c0">If you believe that personal information we hold about you is incorrect, incomplete or inaccurate, then you may ask us to amend it. We will consider if the information requires amendment. If we do not agree that there are grounds for amendment, then we will add a note to the personal information stating that you disagree with it.</span></li> <li class="c3"><span class="c0">Account holders will generally be able to access and update their details online. We request that you keep your information as current as possible so that we may continue to improve our service to you.</span><a id="id.lnxbz9"></a></li> </ol> <p class="c2 c22"> </p><ol class="c4 lst-kix_list_39-0 nitro-offscreen" start="8"> <li class="c8"> <h4 id="h.35nkun2" style="display:inline;"><span class="c5">DELETION OF PERSONAL INFORMATION</span></h4> </li> </ol> <ol class="c4 lst-kix_list_39-1 start nitro-offscreen" start="1"> <li class="c3"><span class="c0">We keep your personal information only as long as we need it for legitimate business purposes (as laid out in&nbsp;</span><span class="c0"><a class="c18" href="https://www.google.com/url?q=https://www.gotinder.com/%23how-we-use-info&amp;sa=D&amp;ust=1606885071276000&amp;usg=AOvVaw0IOiB00YdlpfGKAE1RyZIG" target="_blank" rel="noopener">section 4</a></span><span class="c0">&nbsp;above) and as permitted by applicable law. </span></li> <li class="c3"><span class="c0">Even though our systems are designed to carry out information deletion processes according to the guidelines in paragraphs 8.1 above, we cannot promise that all information will be deleted within a specific timeframe due to technical constraints.</span></li> </ol> <p class="c2 c22"> </p><ol class="c4 lst-kix_list_39-0 nitro-offscreen" start="9"> <li class="c8"> <h4 id="h.1ksv4uv" style="display:inline;"><span class="c6 c26">HOW CAN YOU COMPLAIN ABOUT A BREACH OF PRIVACY? </span></h4> </li> </ol> <ol class="c4 lst-kix_list_39-1 start nitro-offscreen" start="1"> <li class="c3"><span class="c0">If you believe your privacy has been breached by us or have any questions or concerns about our Privacy Policy, please contact us using the contact information below and provide details of the incident / matter so that we can consider / investigate it:</span></li> </ol> <p id="h.44sinio" class="c22 c27 nitro-offscreen"><span class="c5">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;Attention: Privacy Officer</span></p> <p class="c27 c22 nitro-offscreen"><span class="c6">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;Email:</span><span class="c0">&nbsp;ayden-james@viewport.com.au</span></p> <p class="c27 c22 nitro-offscreen"><span class="c6">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;Postal address: </span><span class="c1">Level 1, 222 Queen Victoria Street, North Fremantle 6159</span></p> <ol class="c4 lst-kix_list_39-1 nitro-offscreen" start="2"> <li class="c3"><span class="c0">We have a formal procedure for investigating and dealing with privacy breaches. Once the Privacy Officer receives a complaint in writing the Privacy Officer will commence an investigation. The investigation will endeavour to determine whether there has been a breach, the nature of the breach and how it occurred. We may contact you during the process to seek any further clarification if necessary. If a breach is found, the Privacy Officer will escalate the matter to management so that the process can be rectified to prevent any further breaches from taking place. We will also contact you to inform you of the outcome of the investigation. We will endeavour to resolve all investigations within a reasonable time.</span></li> </ol> <p class="c2 c22"> </p><ol class="c4 lst-kix_list_39-0 nitro-offscreen" start="10"> <li class="c8"> <h4 id="h.2jxsxqh" style="display:inline;"><span class="c5">CHILDRENS PRIVACY</span></h4> </li> </ol> <p class="c10 c15 nitro-offscreen"><span class="c1">We may collect personal information regarding a child under 18 years of age from a parent or legal guardian. You must not provide personal information to us about a child or another person unless you are authorised to do so by law. If you are under 18 years of age and you provide us with your personal information, your parent or legal guardian must approve, on your behalf, the provision of your personal information to us. </span></p> <p class="c2 c15"> </p><ol class="c4 lst-kix_list_39-0 nitro-offscreen" start="11"> <li class="c8"> <h4 id="h.z337ya" style="display:inline;"><span class="c5">USE OF COOKIES </span></h4> </li> </ol> <ol class="c4 lst-kix_list_39-1 start nitro-offscreen" start="1"> <li class="c3"><span class="c0">In some cases, we may collect personal information through the use of cookies. When you access a Platform, we may send a cookie (a small summary file containing a unique ID number) to your computer or device. This enables us to recognise your computer or device and greet you each time you use the Platform, without asking you to register or login. It also helps us keep track of the products or services you view, so that we can send you news about those products or services.</span></li> <li class="c3"><span class="c0">We also use cookies to measure traffic patterns, to determine which Platforms have been visited and to measure other patterns, including transaction patterns, or other metrics in the aggregate. We use this to research your habits so that we can continually improve the Platforms.</span></li> <li class="c3"><span class="c0">We may also use cookies to log IP addresses to analyse trends, administer our Platforms, track user movements, and gather broad demographic information or to collect anonymous data.</span></li> <li class="c3"><span class="c0">If you do not wish to receive cookies, you should set your browser so that your computer or device does not accept them.</span></li> <li class="c3"><span class="c0">We may collect information from you in response to a survey. We generally use this information to get your feedback, report statistics, analyse trends, administer our services, diagnose problems and improve the quality of the Platforms. </span></li> <li class="c3"><span class="c0">If you do not want us to collect information provided by you during the course of a survey, then refrain from completing the survey.</span></li> </ol> <p class="c2 c22"> </p><ol class="c4 lst-kix_list_39-0 nitro-offscreen" start="12"> <li class="c8"> <h4 id="h.3j2qqm3" style="display:inline;"><span class="c5">DIRECT MARKETING </span></h4> </li> </ol> <p class="c10 c15 nitro-offscreen"><span class="c1">We may send you direct marketing communications and information about products and services that we consider may be of interest to you. These communications may be sent in various forms, including mail or email, in accordance with applicable marketing laws, such as the </span><span class="c1 c12">Spam Act 2004</span><span class="c0">&nbsp;(Cth). If you indicate a preference for a method of communication, we will endeavour to use that method whenever practical to do so.</span></p> <p class="c2"> </p><ol class="c4 lst-kix_list_39-0 nitro-offscreen" start="13"> <li class="c8"> <h4 id="h.1y810tw" style="display:inline;"><span class="c5">OFFERS AND PROMOTIONAL MESSAGES</span></h4> </li> </ol> <ol class="c4 lst-kix_list_39-1 start nitro-offscreen" start="1"> <li class="c3"><span class="c0">We may use your email address or mobile phone number to send you updates and communications about our products and services or other messages, such as newsletters, text messages, changes to features of the Platforms, or special offers.</span></li> <li class="c3"><span class="c0">You will be given the opportunity, in any promotional email or text message that we send to you, to opt-out of receiving such messages in the future.</span></li> </ol> <p class="c2"> </p><ol class="c4 lst-kix_list_39-0 nitro-offscreen" start="14"> <li class="c8"> <h4 id="h.4i7ojhp" style="display:inline;"><span class="c5">PUSH NOTIFICATIONS</span></h4> </li> </ol> <ol class="c4 lst-kix_list_39-1 start nitro-offscreen" start="1"> <li class="c3"><span class="c0">Our applications may include a function that allows us to use push notifications to send you updates, communications and other messages about the Platform.</span></li> <li class="c3"><span class="c0">To opt-out of getting these push notifications or other messages you must terminate the applicable service. We do not send promotional messages about other products or services through these push notifications.</span></li> </ol> <p class="c2 c22"> </p><ol class="c4 lst-kix_list_39-0 nitro-offscreen" start="15"> <li class="c8"> <h4 id="h.2xcytpi" style="display:inline;"><span class="c5">THIRD PARTY OFFERS</span></h4> </li> </ol> <ol class="c4 lst-kix_list_39-1 start nitro-offscreen" start="1"> <li class="c3"><span class="c0">We may use the information you have given us about your interests, and other profile or personal information, to develop and display tailored third-party content and advertising.</span></li> <li class="c3"><span class="c0">At any time, you may opt-out of receiving marketing communications from us by contacting us (details at section 9 above) or through the privacy settings on the website or application you are using.</span></li> <li class="c3"><span class="c0">If you receive communications from us that you believe have been sent to you other than in accordance with this Privacy Policy, or in breach of any law, please contact us.</span></li> </ol> <p class="c2 c22"> </p><ol class="c4 lst-kix_list_39-0 nitro-offscreen" start="16"> <li class="c8"> <h4 id="h.1ci93xb" style="display:inline;"><span class="c5">CROSS BRODER DISCLOSURE OF PERSONAL INFORMATION </span></h4> </li> </ol> <ol class="c4 lst-kix_list_39-1 start nitro-offscreen" start="1"> <li class="c3"><span class="c0">The Platforms operate in several international jurisdictions including Australia, New Zealand, the USA and the UK.</span></li> <li class="c3"><span class="c0">As a result, your personal data may be transferred, stored and processed in another country in which we or our subsidiaries, partners or agents maintain facilities. These data processors, acting under our instructions, may be engaged in, among other things, the fulfilment of your information requests and the provision of support tools and services on the Platforms. They may also help us maintain the integrity and security of the Platforms, including emails and messaging services on the Platforms.</span></li> <li class="c3"><span class="c0">By submitting your personal information to us on a Platform (or otherwise), you expressly agree and consent to the disclosure, transfer, storage and processing of your personal information outside Australia. In providing this consent, you understand and acknowledge that countries outside Australia do not always have the same privacy protection obligations as Australia in relation to personal information. However, we will take steps to ensure that your information is used by third-parties securely and in accordance with the terms of our Privacy Policy.</span></li> </ol> <p class="c2 c22"> </p><p class="nitro-offscreen">&nbsp;</p> <ol class="c4 lst-kix_list_39-0 nitro-offscreen" start="17"> <li class="c8"> <h4 id="h.2bn6wsx" style="display:inline;"><span class="c5">SECURITY  HOW WE STORE AND PROTECT YOUR INFORMATION </span></h4> </li> </ol> <ol class="c4 lst-kix_list_39-1 start nitro-offscreen" start="1"> <li class="c3"><span class="c0">We will take reasonable steps to protect the personal information that we hold from misuse, loss, or unauthorised access, including by means of firewalls, password access, secure servers and encryption of credit card transactions.</span></li> <li class="c3"><span class="c0">If you suspect any misuse or loss of, or unauthorised access to, your personal information, please let us know immediately.</span></li> <li class="c3"><span class="c0">In the event that any information under our control is compromised as a result of a breach of security, we will take reasonable steps to investigate the situation and where appropriate, notify those individuals whose information may have been compromised and take other steps, in accordance with any applicable laws and regulations.</span></li> </ol> <p class="c2 c22"> </p><p class="nitro-offscreen">&nbsp;</p> <ol class="c4 lst-kix_list_39-0 nitro-offscreen" start="18"> <li class="c8"> <h4 id="h.3as4poj" style="display:inline;"><span class="c5">LINKS</span></h4> </li> </ol> <p class="c10 c15 nitro-offscreen"><span class="c0">The Platforms may contain links to other websites operated by third-parties. We make no representations or warranties in relation to the privacy practices of any third-party website and we are not responsible for the privacy policies or the content of any third-party website. Third-party websites are responsible for informing you about their own privacy practices.</span></p> <p class="c2 c15"> </p><ol class="c4 lst-kix_list_39-0 nitro-offscreen" start="19"> <li class="c8"> <h4 id="h.1pxezwc" style="display:inline;"><span class="c5">THE SALE OR TRANSFER OF OUR BUSINESS OR ASSETS </span></h4> </li> </ol> <ol class="c4 lst-kix_list_39-1 start nitro-offscreen" start="1"> <li class="c3"><span class="c0">If the business of Viewport is sold or disposed of as a going concern, whether by merger, sale of assets, change of ownership of operating entity or otherwise, or in the event of an insolvency, bankruptcy or receivership, the personal information of our customers may be one of the assets dealt with in connection with that transaction.</span></li> <li class="c3"><span class="c0">Information about our customers may also need to be disclosed in connection with a commercial transaction where we or any of our businesses are seeking finance or investment, support or funding. </span></li> </ol> <p class="c2 c22"> </p><ol class="c4 lst-kix_list_39-0 nitro-offscreen" start="20"> <li class="c8"> <h4 id="h.49x2ik5" style="display:inline;"><span class="c5">ADDITIONAL RIGHTS UNDER EU LAW </span></h4> </li> </ol> <p class="c10 c15 nitro-offscreen"><span class="c5">(This section 20 applies if you are located in the European Union (EU))</span></p> <ol class="c4 lst-kix_list_39-1 nitro-offscreen" start="3"> <li class="c3"><span class="c0">In addition to the rights outlined elsewhere in this Privacy Policy, under certain conditions you may have the right under EU data protection law to ask us to:</span></li> </ol> <ol class="c4 lst-kix_list_37-0 start nitro-offscreen" start="1"> <li class="c7"><span class="c0">provide you with further details on how we use and process your personal information;</span></li> <li class="c7"><span class="c0">delete personal information we no longer have grounds to process; and</span></li> <li class="c7"><span class="c0">restrict how we process your personal information while we consider an enquiry you have raised.</span></li> </ol> <ol class="c4 lst-kix_list_39-1 start nitro-offscreen" start="1"> <li class="c3"><span class="c0">In addition, under certain conditions, you have the right to:</span></li> </ol> <ol class="c4 lst-kix_list_38-0 start nitro-offscreen" start="1"> <li class="c7"><span class="c0">where processing is based on consent, withdraw the consent;</span></li> <li class="c7"><span class="c0">lodge a complaint with the appropriate data protection authority if you have an issue with how we process your personal data;</span></li> <li class="c7"><span class="c0">object to any processing of personal information that we process on the legitimate interests or public interests grounds, unless our reasons for the underlying processing outweighs your interests, rights and freedoms; and</span></li> <li class="c7"><span class="c0">object to direct marketing (including any profiling for such purposes) at any time.</span></li> </ol> <ol class="c4 lst-kix_list_39-1 start nitro-offscreen" start="1"> <li class="c3"><span class="c0">You can exercise these rights by contacting us (details at section 9 above).</span></li> <li class="c3"><span class="c0">These rights are subject to certain exemptions to safeguard the public interest (e.g. the prevention or detection of crime) and our interests (e.g. the maintenance of legal privilege).</span></li> </ol> <div> <p class="c16"> </p><p class="c17"> </p></div> </div></section></main> <script nitro-exclude="">
